Thrilled to announce that I've successfully completed the "
Accounting and
Examination" course offered by West Virginia University.
This course provides tools and techniques for preventing, deterring, detecting, investigating and remediating fraud. It includes different topics such as :
- Identifying common red flags,
- Differentiating between accidental and predator fraudsters, recognizing the nefarious nature and costly impact of the predator fraudster, as well as identifying basic organizational control structures used to prevent fraud,
- Examining evidential matter, both electronic and paper formats including â€œbig dataâ€ to determine the: who, what, when, where and how of fraudulent acts,
- Reviewing the elements involved in money laundering when concealing illicit and illegal sources of financial gain,
- Identifying the characteristics of a whistle-blower and discuss the importance of whistle-blowing as an anti-fraud measure.

Thanks toandfor providing such a great opportunity.

About
About
I have over 17 years experience in executing professional auditing and accounting services in Tunisia. with an accounting background and a graduation in the Chartered Accounting, i integrated KPMG Tunisia in September 2006, where i worked in the Financial Auditing.
Given the office's size and the possibilities of being involved in multi-disciplined teams, i have worked in both the Assurance (IFRS Audit) and Transaction activies in KPMG Tunisia. I have been also involved in various transaction services assignments in Libya, Lebanon and also Djibouti.
During this period, i had the opportunity to work within a KPMG France assurance team for 3 years for the audit of the African Development Bank.

I joined SunGard Global Technology in late 2010 where i am in charge of the management of country monthly accounting close and external reporting matters such as dealing with corporate queries, banking requirements, Tax reporting and compliance, US Gaap reporting, annual reporting for the Group and Sox Sarbanes Oxley compliance.
In SunGard, i am also responsible for analysing key financial information to provide to decision makers within the SunGard group with accurate and timely data.

I'm the founder of United Business Consulting, an audit firm offering since august 2014 audit, assurance, tax, consulting, advisory, corporate finance, and legal services.
